! Title: Mordarski Networks assets filter list
! Description: A uBlock Origin compliant filter list that blocks websites that our company deems bad
! Expires: 5 days
! Last modified: Monday, December 04, 2023 09:42:26 PM UTC
! Homepage: https://github.com/Mordarski-Networks/Mordarski-Networks-assets
! License: https://github.com/Mordarski-Networks/Mordarski-Networks-assets/blob/main/LICENSE
!
! GitHub issues: https://github.com/Mordarski-Networks/Mordarski-Networks-assets/issues
! GitHub pull requests: https://github.com/Mordarski-Networks/Mordarski-Networks-assets/pulls
!
! People & websites that helped me create this list:
! https://letsblock.it/filters/search-results
! https://github.com/letsblockit/letsblockit
! https://github.com/DandelionSprout/adfilt/blob/master/Wiki/SyntaxMeaningsThatAreActuallyHumanReadable.md
! https://github.com/gorhill/uBlock/wiki/Static-filter-syntax

!--- Filter Search Results ---!
! Info: https://github.com/gorhill/uBlock/wiki/Static-filter-syntax#specifichide
! Syntax: example.com##.ad-class

bing.com#?#[id$="results"] cite:has-text(tiktok.com):upward(li)
bing.com#?#a[href*="tiktok.com"]:upward(li[data-idx][style^="width"])
bing.com#?#[id*="video"] > [href*="tiktok.com"]:upward(.dg_u)
bing.com##.news-card[url*="tiktok.com"]
www.google.*##.g:has(a[href*="tiktok.com"])
www.google.*##a[href*="tiktok.com"]:upward(1)
duckduckgo.com##ol.react-results--main a[href*="tiktok.com"]:upward(article)
duckduckgo.com##.tile-wrap a[href*="tiktok.com"]:upward(.tile)
